Wet earwax. Normal body odour. Normal colostrum.
Magnitude: 2.0
Repute: Bad

This is normal for non-Asians. It makes ear-wax wet, sticky, and honey-coloured. It also produces colostrum for breast feeding. People with this gene need to use deodorant to avoid smelling bad, unlike some Asians.

Lower risk of dementia and Alzheimer's disease. Higher good cholesterol.
Magnitude: 2.0

One copy of a longevity gene. This seems to raise HDL ("good") cholesterol, and reduce the risk of dementia and Alzheimer's disease. It may slightly increase longevity. It has been particularly studied in Ashkenazi Jews.
